eighty to 90 percent of the world's poppy , opium and heroin , comes out of afghanistan .	世界上百分之八十到九十的大豆、鴉片和海洛因 , 從阿富汗出來 。
we also see there , of course , terrorism .	我們也看到了 , 當然 , 恐怖主義
this is where al qaeda is staged from .	這是基地組織所在之處 。
we also see a very strong insurgency embedded there .	我們也看到一個非常強烈的動亂嵌在那裏 。
so this terrorism concern is also part of the global commons , and what we must address .	所以 , 這種恐怖主義的擔憂也是全球公有物的一部分 , 以及我們必須要處理的 。
so here we are , 21st century .	所以 , 我們在這裡 , 21世紀
we know our 20thcentury tools are not going to work .	我們知道我們20世紀的工具是行不通的
what should we do ?	我們該怎麼做 ?
i would argue that we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我主張我們不能只靠一把槍支來遞送安全 。
we will not deliver security solely from the barrel of a gun .	我們不能只靠槍支來遞送安全 。
we will need the application of military force .	我們將需要軍事力量的應用 。
when we do it , we must do it well , and competently .	當我們做的時候 , 我們必須要做得很好 , 且要有競爭力 。
but my thesis is , opensource security is about international , interagency , privatepublic connection pulled together by this idea of strategic communication on the internet .	但我的論點是 , 開放式安全是關於國際性的 , 介入性 , 私人的共和國的連結 , 由網路上策略性溝通的這個想法拉扯在一起 。
let me give you a couple of examples of how this works in a positive way .	讓我舉幾個例子來說明這如何以正面的方式運作
this is afghanistan . these are afghan soldiers .	這是阿富汗 , 這些是阿富汗士兵
they are all holding books .	他們都拿著書 。
you should say , " that's odd . i thought i read that this demographic , young men and women in their 20s and 30s , is largely illiterate in afghanistan . "	你應該說: 「 這很奇怪 。 我想我讀到 , 這種人口統計 , 年輕男女在二十、三十多歲時 , 很大程度上是不識字的 , 在阿富汗 。 」
you would be correct .	你會是正確的 。
eightyfive percent cannot read when they enter the security forces of afghanistan .	當他們進入阿富汗的安全部隊時 , 85%無法閱讀 。
why ? because the taliban withheld education during the period of time in which these men and women would have learned to read .	為甚麼呢 ? 因為塔利班在時間內繼承了教育 , 這些男人和女人會學會閱讀 。
so the question is , so , why are they all standing there holding books ?	所以問題是 , 為什麼他們都站在那裡拿著書 ?
the answer is , we are teaching them to read in literacy courses by nato in partnership with private sector entities , in partnership with development agencies .	答案是 , 我們在教導他們在識字課程中讀書 , 由北約和私營機構合作 , 和開發機構合作 。
we've taught well over 200 , 000 afghan security forces to read and write at a basic level .	我們教會了超過二十萬種阿富汗安全部隊 , 以基本的水平閱讀和寫 。
when you can read and write in afghanistan , you will typically put a pen in your pocket .	當你能在阿富汗讀和寫時 , 你通常會在你的口袋裡放一支筆 。
at the ceremonies , when these young men and women graduate , they take that pen with great pride , and put it in their pocket .	在典禮上 , 當這些年輕男女畢業時 , 他們用很棒的驕傲 , 把筆放進口袋裡 。
this is bringing together international — there are 50 nations involved in this mission — interagency — these development agencies — and privatepublic , to take on this kind of security .	這結合了國際--有50個國家參與了這項任務--介入這些發展機構和私人共和國 , 來採取這種安全措施 。
now , we are also teaching them combat skills , of course , but i would argue , opensource security means connecting in ways that create longer lasting security effect .	當然 , 我們也在教導他們戰鬥技巧 , 但我認為 , 開放式安全是指用能創造更長久的安全效應的方式來連結 。
this is a us navy warship .	這是美國海軍戰艦 。
it's called the comfort .	所謂的舒適感
there's a sister ship called the mercy .	有一艘叫 " 慈善 " 的姐妹船 ,
they are hospital ships .	他們是醫院的船隻 。
this one , the comfort , operates throughout the caribbean and the coast of south america conducting patient treatments .	這一個 , 舒適 , 在加勒比海和南美洲的海岸進行病人的治療 。
on a typical cruise , they'll do 400 , 000 patient treatments .	在一般的情況下 , 他們會做四十萬個病人的治療 。
it is crewed not strictly by military but by a combination of humanitarian organizations: operation hope , project smile .	它不被軍隊嚴格排列 , 而是被人道主義組織結合:營運希望 , 微笑 。
other organizations send volunteers .	其他組織發送志工
interagency physicians come out .	介入醫師出來
they're all part of this .	他們都是這方面的一部分 。
to give you one example of the impact this can have , this little boy , eight years old , walked with his mother two days to come to the eye clinic put on by the comfort .	舉個例子 , 這個小男孩 , 八歲 , 和他的母親一起走兩天 , 來到舒適的眼科診所 。
when he was fitted , over his extremely myopic eyes , he suddenly looked up and said , " mama , veo el mundo . "	當他被配合時 , 在他極度神秘的眼神之中 , 他突然抬頭說: 「 媽媽 , veoelmundo 。 」
" mom , i see the world . "	「 媽媽 , 我看到世界 。 」
multiply this by 400 , 000 patient treatments , this privatepublic collaboration with security forces , and you begin to see the power of creating security in a very different way .	將這現象乘以40萬個病人的治療方法 , 這種私人和安全部隊合作 , 你開始看到用非常不同的方式創造安全的力量 。
here you see baseball players .	這裡你看到棒球選手
can you pick out the two us army soldiers in this photograph ?	你能在這張照片中挑出兩位美國軍人嗎 ?
they are the two young men on either side of these young boys . this is part of a series of baseball clinics , where we have explored collaboration between major league baseball , the department of state , who sets up the diplomatic piece of this , military baseball players , who are real soldiers with real skills but participate in this mission , and they put on clinics throughout latin america and the caribbean , in honduras , in nicaragua , in all of the central american and caribbean nations where baseball is so popular , and it creates security .	他們是這兩個年輕的男孩兩邊的男孩 。 這是一系列棒球診所的一部分 , 我們探討了棒球聯盟的合作 , 國務院 , 設立了這方面的外交部 , 軍事棒球選手 , 他們是真正的士兵 , 但參與了這個任務 , 他們在整個拉丁美洲和加勒比海 , 在宏大拉瓜和加拉瓜 , 美國 , 各地 , 各地都是棒球聯盟 , 他們創造了棒球聯盟 。
it shows role models to young men and women about fitness and about life that i would argue help create security for us .	它展示給年輕男女關於健身及人生的榜樣 , 我主張要為我們創造安全 。
another aspect of this partnership is in disaster relief .	這個合作關係的另一個面向是在災難救援中 。
this is a us air force helicopter participating after the tsunami in 2004 which killed 250 , 000 people .	這是一架美國空軍直升機在2004年海嘯後參與 , 造成25萬人死亡 。
in each of these major disasters — the tsunami in 2004 , 250 , 000 dead , the kashmiri earthquake in pakistan , 2005 , 85 , 000 dead , the haitian earthquake , about 300 , 000 dead , more recently the awful earthquaketsunami combination which struck japan and its nuclear industry — in all of these instances , we see partnerships between international actors , interagency , privatepublic working with security forces to respond to this kind of natural disaster .	在每一個重大災難中2004年的海嘯中 , 25萬人死於巴基斯坦的卡許米里地震 , 2005年 , 8萬5千人死於海地地震 , 約有30萬人死於海地震 , 更近期的地震海嘯組合 , 使得日本及其核能產業在所有這些例子中 , 我們看到國際演員之間的合作關係 , 跨部隊 , 私人和安全部隊合作 , 與自然災難 。
so these are examples of this idea of opensource security .	這些都是開放式安全概念的例子 。
we tie it together , increasingly , by doing things like this .	我們透過這樣做來將它綁在一起 。
now , you're looking at this thinking , " ah , admiral , these must be sea lanes of communication , or these might be fiber optic cables . "	現在 , 你看著這個想法: 「 啊 , 阿米羅 , 這些一定是溝通的海道 , 或者這些可能是光纖電纜 。 」
no . this is a graphic of the world according to twitter .	不 。 這是根據推特的圖表 。
purple are tweets . green are geolocation .	紫色是推特 , 綠色是地理分配 。
white is the synthesis .	白色是合成
it's a perfect evocation of that great population survey , the six largest nations in the world in descending order: china , india , facebook , the united states , twitter and indonesia .	這是個完美的進化 , 大眾調查 , 世界上最大的六個國家 , 依照秩序排列:中國、印度、臉書、美國、推特 , 和印尼 。
why do we want to get in these nets ?	我們為什麼要在這些蚊帳裡
why do we want to be involved ?	我們為什麼想要參與 ?
we talked earlier about the arab spring , and the power of all this .	我們先前談到阿拉伯之春 , 以及這一切的力量 。
i'll give you another example , and it's how you move this message .	我再舉一個例子 , 就是你如何移動這個訊息 。
i gave a talk like this in london a while back about this point . i said , as i say to all of you , i'm on facebook . friend me .	我在倫敦做過這樣的演講 , 前陣子提到這個時點 。 我說 , 如同我對你們說的 , 我在臉書上 , 朋友我一樣 。
got a little laugh from the audience .	得到觀眾的笑聲 。
there was an article which was run by ap , on the wire .	當時有一篇文章由ap經營 , 在鐵絲網上
got picked up in two places in the world: finland and indonesia .	被發現在世界上兩個地方:芬蘭和印尼 。
the headline was: nato admiral needs friends .	標題是:北約組織需要朋友 。
and the story was a catalyst , and the next morning i had hundreds of facebook friend requests from indonesians and finns , mostly saying , " admiral , we heard you need a friend , and oh , by the way , what is nato ? "	故事是催化劑 , 隔天早上我有上百個facebook好友請求 , 來自印尼人和芬蘭人 , 大部分都會說: 「 阿道德 , 我們聽到你需要一個朋友 , 喔 , 順便說一下 , nato是什麼 ? 」
yeah , we laugh , but this is how we move the message , and moving that message is how we connect international , interagency , privatepublic , and these social nets to help create security .	沒錯 , 我們笑了 , 但這是我們移動訊息的方式 , 移動那訊息是我們如何連結國際、介入、私人共和國 , 以及這些社交網 , 來協助創造安全 。
now , let me hit a somber note .	現在 , 讓我按一個11月的音符
this is a photograph of a brave british soldier .	這是一張勇敢的英國士兵的照片 。
he's in the scots guards .	他在蘇格蘭警衛隊
he's standing the watch in helmand , in southern afghanistan .	他站在helmand , 在阿富汗南部 ,
i put him here to remind us , i would not want anyone to leave the room thinking that we do not need capable , competent militaries who can create real military effect .	我把他放到這裡來提醒我們 , 我不會希望任何人離開房間 , 認為我們不需要有能力、有能力的軍隊 , 能夠創造出真正的軍事效應 。
that is the core of who we are and what we do , and we do it to protect freedom , freedom of speech , all the things we treasure in our societies .	那是我們是誰以及我們所做的事的核心 , 我們為了保護自由 , 言論自由 , 所有我們在社會中珍視的事物 。
but , you know , life is not an onandoff switch .	但 , 你知道的 , 人生不是一個大開關 。
you don't have to have a military that is either in hard combat or is in the barracks .	你不需要有軍隊要麼在艱難的戰鬥中 , 要麼就在巴拉克 。
i would argue life is a rheostat .	我會主張生命是旋律 。
you have to dial it in , and as i think about how we create security in this 21st century , there will be times when we will apply hard power in true war and crisis , but there will be many instances , as we've talked about today , where our militaries can be part of creating 21stcentury security , international , interagency , privatepublic , connected with competent communication .	你得要把它撥入其中 , 正如我所想的 , 我們在這二十一世紀如何創造安全 , 有時候 , 我們會在真正的戰爭和危機中施加硬實力 , 但有許多的例子 , 正如我們今天談到的 , 我們的軍隊可以參與創造二十一世紀的安全 , 國際 , 國際 , 介入 , 私人交流 , 和互相連結 。
i would close by saying that we heard earlier today about wikipedia . i use wikipedia all the time to look up facts , and as all of you appreciate , wikipedia is not created by 12 brilliant people locked in a room writing articles .	最後我會說今天早些時候我們聽到維基百科 。 我常常用維基百科去查證事實 , 正如你們所有人所欣賞的 , 維基百科並不是由12個聰明人所創造出來的 , 被關在一個房間裡寫文章中 。
wikipedia , every day , is tens of thousands of people inputting information , and every day millions of people withdrawing that information .	維基百科 , 每天都有成千上萬的人在輸入資訊 , 每一天都有數百萬人在吸收那些資訊 。
it's a perfect image for the fundamental point that no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	這是個完美的圖像 , 對於根本的重點來說 , 沒有人和所有人一起想的一樣聰明 。
no one person , no one alliance , no one nation , no one of us is as smart as all of us thinking together .	沒有一個人 , 沒有一個同盟國 , 沒有一個國家 , 沒有一個人和我們一起想的一樣聰明 。
the vision statement of wikipedia is very simple: a world in which every human being can freely share in the sum of all knowledge .	維基百科的陳述很簡單:一個每個人可以自由地分享在所有知識的總和中的世界 。
my thesis for you is that by combining international , interagency , privatepublic , strategic communication , together , in this 21st century , we can create the sum of all security .	我的論點是 , 透過結合國際、介入、私人公開、策略性的溝通 , 一起合作 , 在21世紀 , 我們可以創造出所有安全的總和 。
thank you very much . thank you . thank you .	非常感謝 。 謝謝 。 謝謝 。
